</th>

<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1872&#160;; 1879 (orchestra)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Funeral_marches&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Funeral marches</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Funeral_music&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Funeral music</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_piano&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the piano</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_1_player&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 1 player</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_horn%2C_2_trumpets%2C_trombone%2C_tuba_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For horn, 2 trumpets, trombone, tuba (arr)</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Popularized both by the addition of the words "The worms crawl in and the worms crawl out..." and by its use as the theme for "Alfred Hitchcock presents..."
</p>
